-- MIB File for IP Unity Media Server 
-- $Id: IpUnity.mib,v 1.118 2008/08/20 14:49:05 harishn Exp $ 
--

IPUNITY-MEDIA-SERVER-MIB DEFINITIONS ::= BEGIN

IMPORTS  
	enterprises,
	MODULE-IDENTITY,
	OBJECT-TYPE,
	Integer32,
	Counter32,
	IpAddress,
	NOTIFICATION-TYPE
		FROM SNMPv2-SMI
	DisplayString,
	RowStatus
		FROM SNMPv2-TC
	ifIndex
		FROM RFC1213-MIB;

ipUnityMediaServer      MODULE-IDENTITY
    LAST-UPDATED "0408272000Z"  -- 2004, Aug 26 8.00PM GMT
    ORGANIZATION "IP Unity Inc."
    CONTACT-INFO
                 "Technical Support

                Postal: IP Unity Inc.
                        475 Sycamore Drive, Milpitas, CA 95035

                Tel:    1-408-582-1100
                E-Mail: techsupport@ip-unity.com"
    DESCRIPTION
        "The MIB tree for IP Unity under the enterprises node. It describes the 
	IP Unity Proprietary Information in order to manage the IP Unity Media Server."
    ::= { ipunity 1 }

ipunity     OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { enterprises 5134 }

-- Textual conventions 

SccIfType ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Interface type for SCC card."
    SYNTAX INTEGER { other (0),
    				 signal-media (1), 
    				 file-system (2),
    				 management (3), 
    				 signal-cp-only (4), 
    				 signal-application-only (5) 
    } 
    
Language ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Possible languages"
    SYNTAX INTEGER { 
    	english (1), 
    	chinese (2), 
    	spanish (3),
    	japanese (4),
    	french (5),
    	russian (6),
        german (7),
        swedish (8),
        malay (9),
        tamil (10),
        dutch (11)
    }
    
ITUAdminState ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the various possible administrative states (ITU-T X.731)"
    SYNTAX INTEGER { 
    	locked (0), 
       	unlocked (1),
    	shuttingDown (2) 
    }

ITUOperState ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the various possible operational states (ITU-T X.731)"
    SYNTAX INTEGER { 
    	disabled (0), 
       	enabled (1)
	}

ITUUsageState ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the various possible usage states (ITU-T X.731)"
    SYNTAX INTEGER { 
    	idle (0), 
       	active (1),
       	busy (2),
       	initializing (3),
       	init-failed (4),
       	enabling (5),
       	disabling (6),
       	annc-download (7)
	}

ITUAvailabilityStatus ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the various possible availability status values
		(ITU-T X.731)."
    SYNTAX INTEGER { 
		not-installed(0),
		installed(1),
		in-test(2),
		power-off(3),
		off-duty(4),
		in-sync(5),
		init-failed(6)
	}
	
ITUStandbyStatus ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the various possible standby status values
		(ITU-T X.731)."
    SYNTAX INTEGER {
		not-applicapble(0),
		not-available (1),
		providing-service (2),
		cold-standby (3),
		hot-standby (4),
		warm-standby (5)
	}
	
MtceAdminCommand ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Used for providing the administration related maintenance 
		command."
    SYNTAX INTEGER {
                no-command (0),
		lock-graceful (1),
		lock-force (2),
		unlock (3),
		reset (4)     
	}

MtceAdminCommandStatus ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Used for providing the result of MtceAdminCommand."
    SYNTAX INTEGER {
		null (0),
		in-progress (1),
		success (2),     
		failed (3),
		rejected (4)
	}					        

LanguageBitMap ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Used for providing the bit map representation of the language supported.
		It will be represented in the 2 power n values based on the languages.
		Following are the currently supported value.
                1 ------ none
		2(2^1) - English
		4(2^2) - Chinese
	        8(2^3) - Spanish	
		16(2^4) - Japanese
	        32(2^5) - French	
		64(2^6) - Russian
	        128(2^7) - German	
	        256(2^8) - Swedish	
	        512(2^9) - Malay	
		1024(2^10) - Tamil
	        2048(2^11) - Dutch."
    SYNTAX Integer32	

IPv6SupportIfType ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"Interface type support for IPv6."
    SYNTAX INTEGER { 
    				 signal-media (1)
    } 
    
-- Type definitions for card , bank , module , channel numbers

IpUnityCardNo  		::= INTEGER (0..9 | 0..3)
IpUnityBankNo		::= INTEGER (0..3)
IpUnityModuleNo		::= INTEGER (0..7)
IpUnityChannelNo	::= INTEGER (0..31)

-- OBJECT IDENTIFIER Definitions:

ipUnityMSConfigMib      	OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 1 }
ipUnityStatistics       	OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 2 }
ipUnityMaintenanceGroup    	OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 3 }
ipUnityNotificationPrefix	OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 4 }
ipUnityTrapRelatedVariables	OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 5 } 
msConfigurationObjects		OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 6 }
msSecurityObjects		OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 7 }
ipUnityBannerGroup		OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 8 }
ipUnitySoftwareLicenseGroup	OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityMediaServer 9 }

ipUnityNotifications		OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { ipUnityNotificationPrefix 0 }

-- IP Unity Media Server Configuration MIB objects   
-- Obsoleting this entire group. 
-- All the configuration objects will be present in 
-- msConfigurationObjects group with proper hierarchy for Media Server release 2.7 onwards.

-- ipUnityMSConfigMib is OBSOLETE
-- ipSecEthernetModeTable is OBSOLETE and is replaced with ipSecEtherModeTable



-- the IP Unity card table

ipUnityCardTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityCardEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"A table containing information for each card in the Media Server.
		An entry will be present whether the card is present in the slot
		or not."
	::= { ipUnityMaintenanceGroup 1 }

ipUnityCardEntry OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityCardEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"An entry in the card table containing information about a
		particular card."
    INDEX { ipUnityCardIndex }
	::= { ipUnityCardTable  1 }

IpUnityCardEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityCardIndex				IpUnityCardNo,
	ipUnityCardType					INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardAdminState			ITUAdminState,
	ipUnityCardOperState			ITUOperState,
	ipUnityCardUsageState			ITUUsageState,
	ipUnityCardAvailabilityStatus	ITUAvailabilityStatus,
	ipUnityCardStandbyStatus		ITUStandbyStatus,
	ipUnityCardNumCriticalAlarms	INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardNumMajorAlarms		INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardNumMinorAlarms		INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardManfacType			INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardAdminCommand			MtceAdminCommand,
	ipUnityCardAdminCommandStatus	MtceAdminCommandStatus,
	ipUnityCardAdminCmdFailureReason	DisplayString,
	ipUnityCardCpuUsage			INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardMemUsage			INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardAvgCpuUsage			INTEGER,
	ipUnityCardAvgMemUsage			INTEGER
}

ipUnityCardIndex OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityCardNo
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the Card number."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 1 }

ipUnityCardType OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		other (0),
		scc (1),
		mpc (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only 
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the type of the Card. This is the basic card type.
		Manufacturing type of the card gives the actual hardware type for
		the card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 2 }

ipUnityCardAdminState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUAdminState
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU administrative state of the Card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 3 }

ipUnityCardOperState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUOperState
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU operational state of the Card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 4 }
		
ipUnityCardUsageState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUUsageState
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU usage state of the Card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 5 }

ipUnityCardAvailabilityStatus OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUAvailabilityStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU availability status of the card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 6 }
        
ipUnityCardStandbyStatus OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUStandbyStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU standby status of the card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 7 }

ipUnityCardNumCriticalAlarms OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER	(0..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the number of critical alarms generated by this card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 8 }
        
ipUnityCardNumMajorAlarms OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER	(0..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		" Represents the number of major alarms generated by this card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 9 }
        
ipUnityCardNumMinorAlarms OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER	(0..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the number of minor alarms generated by this card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 10 }
	
ipUnityCardManfacType OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		other (0),
		mpc1 (1),
		mpc2 (2),
		mpc4 (4),
		spm (5),
		scc1 (10),
		mpc11 (11),
		mpc12 (12),
		mpc14 (14),
		mpc15 (15),
		mpc16 (16),
		mpc17 (17),
		mpc18 (18),
		scc2 (20),
		scc3 (30),
		mpc20 (31)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Gives the manufacturing type for the card."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 11 } 	

ipUnityCardAdminCommand OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX MtceAdminCommand
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Used by the adminstrator to lock, unlock or reset the card. Each 
		operation may take good amount of time so the management station needs
		to query the ipUnityCardAdminCommandStatus object to know the result
		of the command set through this object.
		
		At a time only one command is allowed. MediaServer won't accept any
		command until the current command is completed. If management station
		sends another command when the first command is in-progress then Media
		Server rejects the second command immediatley.
		
		For get operation this object returns the last command that has been
		executed for this card through SNMP interface."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 12 }

ipUnityCardAdminCommandStatus OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX MtceAdminCommandStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Status of the command ipUnityCardAdminCommand."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 13 }	

ipUnityCardAdminCmdFailureReason OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Result of the command ipUnityCardAdminCommand. This value
                 is to give extra error information on why ipUnityCardAdminCommand
                 is failed. "
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 14 }		

ipUnityCardCpuUsage OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX INTEGER
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Cpu Usage by this card.The value -1 indicates invalid usage."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 15 }

ipUnityCardMemUsage OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Memory Usage by this card.The value -1 indicates invalid usage."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 16 }

ipUnityCardAvgCpuUsage OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Average CPU usage by this card.The value -1 indicates invalid usage."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 17 }

ipUnityCardAvgMemUsage OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Average Memory usage by this card.The value -1 indicates invalid usage."
	::= {ipUnityCardEntry 18 }

-- the IP Unity bank table 

ipUnityBankTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityBankEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		" A table containing information about each ODSP bank in the 
		Media Server." 
	::= { ipUnityMaintenanceGroup 2 }

ipUnityBankEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityBankEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"An entry in the bank table containing information about the current 
		status of the bank."
	INDEX { ipUnityCardIndex, ipUnityBankIndex }
	::= { ipUnityBankTable  1 }

IpUnityBankEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityBankIndex      			IpUnityBankNo,
	ipUnityBankType					INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankAddress       		IpAddress,
	ipUnityBankAdminState 			ITUAdminState,
	ipUnityBankOperState 			ITUOperState,
	ipUnityBankUsageState			ITUUsageState,
	ipUnityBankAvailabilityStatus	ITUAvailabilityStatus,
	ipUnityBankNumCriticalAlarms	INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankNumMajorAlarms		INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankNumMinorAlarms		INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankOdspImageVersion		DisplayString,
	ipUnityBankAdminCommand			MtceAdminCommand,
	ipUnityBankAdminCommandStatus	MtceAdminCommandStatus,
	ipUnityBankAdminCmdFailureReason	DisplayString,
	ipUnityBankCpuUsage			INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankMemUsage			INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankAvgCpuUsage			INTEGER,
	ipUnityBankAvgMemUsage			INTEGER
}

ipUnityBankIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX IpUnityBankNo
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "Represents the bank number."
        ::= {ipUnityBankEntry 1 }

ipUnityBankType OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		unknown (0),
		odsp (1),
		odsp2 (2),
		spm (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only 
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the type of the bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 2 }

ipUnityBankAddress OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpAddress
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the IP address of the bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 3 }

ipUnityBankAdminState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUAdminState
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU administrative state of the Bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 4 }

ipUnityBankOperState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUOperState
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU operational state of the Bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 5 }
		
ipUnityBankUsageState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUUsageState
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU usage state of the Bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 6 }

ipUnityBankAvailabilityStatus OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUAvailabilityStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the current ITU availability status of the bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 7 }
        
ipUnityBankNumCriticalAlarms OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER	(0..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		" Represents the number of critical alarms generated by this bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 8 }
        
ipUnityBankNumMajorAlarms OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER	(0..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		" Represents the number of major alarms generated by this bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 9 }
        
ipUnityBankNumMinorAlarms OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER	(0..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		" Represents the number of minor alarms generated by this bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 10 }
        
ipUnityBankOdspImageVersion OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS obsolete
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the version of the software image running in the bank."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 11 }

ipUnityBankAdminCommand OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX MtceAdminCommand
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Used by the adminstrator to lock, unlock or reset the bank. Each 
		operation may take good amount of time so the management station needs
		to query the ipUnityBankAdminCommandStatus object to know the result
		of the command set through this object.
		
		At a time only one command is allowed. MediaServer won't accept any
		command until the current command is completed. If management station
		sends another command when the first command is in-progress then Media
		Server rejects the second command immediatley.
		
		For get operation this object returns the last command that has been
		executed for this card through SNMP interface."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 12 }

ipUnityBankAdminCommandStatus OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX MtceAdminCommandStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Status of the command ipUnityBankAdminCommand."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 13 }		

ipUnityBankAdminCmdFailureReason OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Result of the command ipUnityBankAdminCommand. This value
                 is to give extra error information on why ipUnityBankAdminCommand
                 is failed."
	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 14 }

	SYNTAX INTEGER
	MAX-ACCESS read-only

	::= {ipUnityBankEntry 18 }

-- the IP Unity module table

ipUnityModuleTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityModuleEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"A table containing information on the DSP module configuration in a bank 
		in the Media Server."
	::= { ipUnityMaintenanceGroup 3 }

ipUnityModuleEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IpUnityModuleEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"An entry in the module table containing information about the current 
		configuration of the module."
    INDEX { ipUnityCardIndex, ipUnityBankIndex, ipUnityModuleIndex }
    ::= { ipUnityModuleTable  1 }

IpUnityModuleEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityModuleIndex      		IpUnityModuleNo,
	ipUnityModuleAdminState 		ITUAdminState,
	ipUnityModuleOperState 			ITUOperState,
	ipUnityModuleUsageState			ITUUsageState,
	ipUnityModuleAvailabilityStatus	ITUAvailabilityStatus,
	ipUnityModuleNumCriticalAlarms	INTEGER,
	ipUnityModuleNumMajorAlarms		INTEGER,
	ipUnityModuleNumMinorAlarms		INTEGER,
	ipUnityModuleDspImageVersion	DisplayString,
	ipUnityModuleAppType 			INTEGER,
	ipUnityModuleAdminCommand		MtceAdminCommand,
	ipUnityModuleAdminCommandStatus	MtceAdminCommandStatus,
	ipUnityModuleAdminCmdFailureReason	DisplayString,
    ipUnityModuleCpuUsage         INTEGER,
    ipUnityModuleMemUsage         INTEGER,
    ipUnityModuleAvgCpuUsage          INTEGER,
    ipUnityModuleAvgMemUsage          INTEGER
}

ipUnityModuleIndex OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityModuleNo
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the module number."
	::= {ipUnityModuleEntry 1 }

ipUnityModuleAdminState OBJECT-TYPE

	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current

ipUnityModuleUsageState OBJECT-TYPE

	STATUS current

	::= {ipUnityModuleEntry 4 }

ipUnityModuleAvailabilityStatus	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ITUAvailabilityStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

ipUnityModuleNumCriticalAlarms	OBJECT-TYPE

	MAX-ACCESS read-only

		" Represents the number of minor alarms generated by this module."

ipUnityModuleDspImageVersion OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

	::= {ipUnityModuleEntry 9 }

ipUnityModuleAppType OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		unknown (0),
		dsp (1),
		dsp2 (2),
		asr (3),

		scc-cp (6),
		asr-icm (7)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Gives the application type for this module."
	::= {ipUnityModuleEntry 10 }

	SYNTAX MtceAdminCommand
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

		operation may take good amount of time so the management station needs

-- the IP Unity DSP channel table
ipUnityChannelTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityChannelEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"A table containing information on the channel configuration in a DSP 
		module in the Media Server."
	::= { ipUnityMaintenanceGroup 4 }

ipUnityChannelEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityChannelEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"An entry in the channel table containing information about the 
		channel."
    INDEX { ipUnityCardIndex, 
    		ipUnityBankIndex, 
    		ipUnityModuleIndex, 
    		ipUnityChannelIndex 
    }
    ::= { ipUnityChannelTable  1 }

IpUnityChannelEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
   ipUnityChannelIndex	IpUnityChannelNo,
   ipUnityChannelState	INTEGER
}

	SYNTAX IpUnityChannelNo
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the channel number."
	::= {ipUnityChannelEntry 1 }

	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		disabled (0),
		idle (1),
		busy (2),
		reserved (3),
		lockUp (4)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only 
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Gives the state of the channel."
	::= {ipUnityChannelEntry 2 }

		off (0),
		on (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Used to set audit off or on."
	::= { msMtceObjects 1 }
	
msMtceSysCommand OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		no-command (0),
		reset (1),
		shutDown (2),
		switchover (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Supported commands are reset, shutDown and switchover. For Get request it 
                 returns no-command(0)."
	::= { msMtceObjects 2 }

msMtceSccStandbyCommand OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		no-command (0),
		shutDown (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Used for shutDown the standby SCC. For Get request it returns no-command(0)."
	::= { msMtceObjects 3 }

	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		no-command (0),
		configuration (1),
		audio-files (2),
		images (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Synchronization command and its options. For Get request it returns no-command(0)."
	::= { msMtceObjects 4 }

msMtceTerminateCommand OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		no-command (0),
		rlogin (1),
		telnet (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"To terminate rlogin/telnet sessions of the Media Server. For Get request it returns 
                 no-command(0). For telnet(2) it won't terminate the CLI sessions it terminates the
                 telnet sessions for ports otherthan 23."
	::= { msMtceObjects 5 }		

msMtceCommandFailureReason OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX DisplayString
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "Failure reason for the last maintainence Command SET by SNMP. The command can be
                 msMtceSccSyncCommand, msMtceTerminateCommand, msMtceSysCommand and
                 msMtceSccStandbyCommand. This string gives the reason for failure."
        ::= { msMtceObjects 6 }

-- Upgrade related objects
imageType OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		none (0),
		bulk (2),
		dsp (3),
		odsp (6),
		spm (9),
		vxml (10),
		scc(12),
		mpcTwenty(13)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Type of the image. Gives what kind of image to upgrade.  
		When this object is not set agent returns none(0)."
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 1 }

imagePath OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"file name and path of the image."
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 2 }

imageHostName OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString (SIZE(1..64))
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Hostname or the IP address on which the image is present. "
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 3 }

imageLogin OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString (SIZE(1..32))
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Login name for imageHostName. "
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 4 }

imageLoginPassword OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString (SIZE(1..32))
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Password for the login name imageLogin. "
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 5 }	
	
imageUpgradeCommand OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
                no-command (0),
		upload (1),
		cancel (2),
		commit (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Command for performing image upgrade. Explanation of each command 
		is as follows
		
		upload - Values for all the read-write scalar 
		variables in this group needs to have correct values to 
		perform the image upload operation. Upload can take some time, 
		so the status can be known by querying imageUploadStatus object.
		
		cancel - Once upload is done then user has a choice to cancel it, if
		he would like to use the old image instead of upgrade. This cancels 
		the upgrade for imageType. It is management station's responsibility
		to make sure imageType is set correctly before performing this
		operation.
		
		commit - User is happy with the image and commiting it. This commits
		the upgrade for imageType. It is management station's responsibility
		to make sure imageType is set correctly before performing this operation.
		
		For Get operation this object returns the last command that has been 
		Set."
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 6 }

imageUploadStatus OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
                no-command (0),
		inprogress (1),
		success (2),
		failed (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Status of the current or last upload procedure. If there is no 
		upgrade in progress then it return the status of the last 
		upgrade. "
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 7 }	 		

upgradeCmdFailureReason OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Failure reason for the last imageUpgradeCommand. This value is useful only
		when imageUploadStatus is failed (3). This string gives the reason for failure."
	::= { msUpgradeObjects 8 }

-- The IP Unity Fan Status Table

ipUnityFanStatusTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityFanStatusEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"A table containing status information of each fan in the Media Server."
	::= { ipUnityMSChassisObjects 27 }

ipUnityFanStatusEntry OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityFanStatusEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"An entry in the fan table containing information about the fan status."
    INDEX { ipUnityFanStatusIndex }
	::= { ipUnityFanStatusTable  1 }

IpUnityFanStatusEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityFanStatusIndex				Integer32,
	ipUnityFanStatusVal				INTEGER
}

ipUnityFanStatusIndex OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Represents the Fan number."
	::= {ipUnityFanStatusEntry 1 }

ipUnityFanStatusVal OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		down (0),
		up (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only 
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		" Represents the Fan status."
	::= {ipUnityFanStatusEntry 2 }

ipUnityOutstandingAlarmTable            OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS current	
        DESCRIPTION
        "The table is used get the outstanding alarm list."
        ::= { ipUnityMaintenanceGroup 9 }

ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX IpUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	        "An entry for each outstanding alarm."
        INDEX { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmIndex }
        ::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmTable 1 }

IpUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry  ::= SEQUENCE {
        ipUnityOutstandingAlarmIndex    	Integer32,
	ipUnityAlarmName			DisplayString,
        ipUnitySeverityLevel                   	INTEGER,
        ipUnityCardNum                         	Integer32,
        ipUnityBankNum                 		Integer32,
        ipUnityModuleNum             	 	Integer32,
        ipUnityChannelNum             		Integer32,
        ipUnityAlarmTimestamp      	 	DisplayString,
        ipUnitySeqNum                    	Integer32,
        ipUnityAlarmString               	DisplayString,
        ipUnityAlarmAdditionalInfoString        DisplayString,
        ipUnityAlarmAdditionalInfoInt           Integer32	
}

ipUnityOutstandingAlarmIndex    OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Outstanding Alarm Index."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 1 }


ipUnityAlarmName OBJECT-TYPE
  	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The Alarm Name."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 2 }
	
ipUnitySeverityLevel OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX      INTEGER {
	      clear (1),
	      informational (2),
	      warning (3),
	      minor (4),
	      major (5),
	      critical (6)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Trap severity level."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 3 }

ipUnityCardNum  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	    "Card Number."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 4 }

ipUnityBankNum OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	    "Bank Number."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 5 }

ipUnityModuleNum OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	    "Module Number."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 6 }

ipUnityChannelNum OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	     "Channel Number."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 7 }

ipUnityAlarmTimestamp    OBJECT-TYPE
  	SYNTAX DisplayString
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	     "The time of occurance of the trap."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 8 }

ipUnitySeqNum   OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	     "The sequence number associated with the alarm."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 9 }

ipUnityAlarmString OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	    "The Alarm String."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 10 }

ipUnityAlarmAdditionalInfoString OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	     "This object gives the additional info string based on the trap and can hold any one of the following strings,
	      ipUnitySccTaskName OR ipUnitySccFileSystemName OR pUnitySccLogFileName OR ipUnityOdspTaskName
	      OR ipUnityOdspLogFileName OR ipUnityTaskName OR ipUnityLogFileName. This object will report null in the absence of 
	      additional string value. "
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 11 }

ipUnityAlarmAdditionalInfoInt OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	    "This object gives the additional info integer value based on the trap and can hold values for any one of the 
	     following additional info. ipUnityFanNumber OR ipUnityPowerSupplyType OR ipUnitySystemTemperature
	     This object will report .-1. in the absence of any additional info integer value."
	::= { ipUnityOutstandingAlarmEntry 12 }

        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION " A table containing partition resource in the Media Server."
 ::= { ipUnityResourceStatistics 5 }

ipUnityPartitionLevelResourceStatisticsEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IpUnityPartitionLevelResourceStatisticsEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
        "An entry in the resource statistics table."
    INDEX      { ipUnityPartitionIndex, ipUnityPartitionResourceType }
    ::= { ipUnityPartitionLevelResourceStatisticsTable  1 }

IpUnityPartitionLevelResourceStatisticsEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
		ipUnityNumBusyChannels                 Integer32,
		ipUnityNumTotalConfiguredChannels      Integer32
}

ipUnityNumBusyChannels 	OBJECT-TYPE        
        SYNTAX Integer32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION		"Total number of busy channels for a partition."
::= { ipUnityPartitionLevelResourceStatisticsEntry 1 }

ipUnityNumTotalConfiguredChannels 	OBJECT-TYPE        
        SYNTAX Integer32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION		"Total number of configured channels for a partition."
::= { ipUnityPartitionLevelResourceStatisticsEntry 2 }

-- HTTP server table statistics

ipUnityHttpServerTable		OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityHttpServerEntry
        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The table containing the HTTP server related data."
	::= { ipUnityHttpServerStatistics 1 }

ipUnityHttpServerEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IpUnityHttpServerEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
        	"An entry in the HTTP server related data table containing the set of 
		data for that server."
    INDEX      { ipUnityHttpServerAddress }
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerTable 1 }

IpUnityHttpServerEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityHttpServerAddress			IpAddress,
	ipUnityHttpServerConnectionFailures		Counter32,
	ipUnityHttpServerUnexpectedConnectionCloses	Counter32,
	ipUnityHttpServerFetches			Counter32,
	ipUnityHttpServerFetchErrors			Counter32,
	ipUnityHttpServerAverageThroughput		Integer32,
	ipUnityHttpServerRejectionsForPlayingAnnc	Counter32,
	ipUnityHttpServerStreamingBufferUnderruns	Counter32
	}

ipUnityHttpServerAddress	OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX IpAddress	
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The IP Address of HTTP Server."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 1 }

ipUnityHttpServerConnectionFailures	OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX Counter32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The number of connection failures for this HTTP server."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 2 }

ipUnityHttpServerUnexpectedConnectionCloses	OBJECT-TYPE
        SYNTAX 	Counter32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The number of unexpected HTTP connection closes done by the server."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 3 }

ipUnityHttpServerFetches	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX 	Counter32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The number of HTTP fetches initiated on this server."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 4 }

ipUnityHttpServerFetchErrors	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX 	Counter32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The number of fetch errors at this HTTP Server."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 5 }

ipUnityHttpServerAverageThroughput	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	Integer32
	UNITS	"kilobits per second"
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The Average Throughput on this HTTP server in kilobits per second."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 6 }

ipUnityHttpServerRejectionsForPlayingAnnc	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	Counter32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The number of times announcement playing from this HTTP server was rejected."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 7 }

ipUnityHttpServerStreamingBufferUnderruns	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX	Counter32
        MAX-ACCESS read-only
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
                "The number of times there were streaming buffer (pre-play buffer) underruns 
		while playing from this server."
    ::= { ipUnityHttpServerEntry 8 }

ipUnityHostNameTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityHostNameEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The table contains hostname configuration info."
	::= { nodeConfig 11 }

ipUnityHostNameEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX IpUnityHostNameEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"An entry for hostname details."
    INDEX { ipUnityHostNameIndex }
    ::= { ipUnityHostNameTable 1 }

IpUnityHostNameEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityHostNameIndex		Integer32,
	ipUnityHostName  	        DisplayString,
	ipUnityHostNameType		INTEGER,
	ipUnityHostNameRowStatus	RowStatus
	}

ipUnityHostNameIndex	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32 (0..5)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"HostName entry number in the table."
    ::= { ipUnityHostNameEntry 1 }

ipUnityHostName	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Host name."
    ::= { ipUnityHostNameEntry 2 }

ipUnityHostNameType	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		signal-media (0),
		mgmt (1),
		nfs (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Hostname Type:  signal-media, mgmt or nfs."
    ::= { ipUnityHostNameEntry 3 }    

ipUnityHostNameRowStatus    OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX RowStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The status of the row. Required to create or delete the entry in 
		this table. Only createAndGo method of row creation is supported 
		and createAndWait method is not supported."
	::= { ipUnityHostNameEntry 4 }

languageList OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX OCTET STRING (SIZE (1..3))
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"List of the languages. one byte for each language. Byte value 
		takes one value from the Language enumeration defined in 
		Textual conventions. User can set one, two or three languages in
		the list. Same language can not be repeated.
		
		Some Excamples or
		  a) English(1), Spanish(3)                 (0x01 0x03)
		  b) Chinese(2), English(1), Spanish(3)     (0x02 0x01 0x03)
		  c) Russian(6)                             (0x06)
		."
	::= { sysConfig 12 }

historyLog	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		off (0),
		on (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Turn History Logging off or on."

configErrStringTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF ConfigErrStringEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The table contains Error information for latest set request."
	::= { sysConfig 20 }

configErrStringEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX ConfigErrStringEntry
        MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
		"An entry per one error string"
        INDEX      { configErrIndex }
        ::= { configErrStringTable 1 }

ConfigErrStringEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	configErrIndex			Integer32,
	configErrString			DisplayString
	}
    
configErrIndex	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32 (0..9)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
        STATUS current
        DESCRIPTION
		"Index for this table. Atmost a set request will have 10 error strings"
        ::= { configErrStringEntry 1 }

configErrString OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Error string that gives the reason for latest SNMP set failure.  
		When a SNMP Set request fails this string gives the reason
		for its failure.

		For all standard failures like noSuchName, bad value etc 
		management station should depend on error status field
		in the response.
	
		This string is updated for non SNMP standard errors. For
		any reason if error can not be determined by the agent then 
		agent returns null string (0 length).

		This string gives the result of the latest SNMP set request 
		that is handled by the agent. It is management station's 
		responsibility to read the result before performing another 
		SET operation." 
	::= { configErrStringEntry 2 }

	        major (5),
	        critical (6),
	        all(10)	
    }
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
                "This object allows to generate traps for the outstanding alarms
	based on the severity set. Traps will be sent out to all the registered snmp
        managers for the corresponding outstanding alarms based on the severity value
        set in the object."
	::= { sysConfig 24 }

		that are configured. Same table is also used to remove the announcement
		instructions, however user can only mark the entries to remove. Actual
		deletion happens when user does the save operation using ipUnityAnncInstCommand
	        when all the odsp banks are OutOfService.The entries in the user change can only
                be modified."
	::= { ipUnityAnncConfig 4 }

ipUnityAnncInstEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IpUnityAnncInstEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"An entry for announcement instruction."
    INDEX      { ipUnityAnncInstIndex }
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstTable 1 }

IpUnityAnncInstEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityAnncInstIndex	        Integer32,
	ipUnityAnncInstSectionType	INTEGER,
	ipUnityAnncInstDesignation	INTEGER,
        ipUnityAnncInstType	        INTEGER,
        ipUnityAnncInstDynamicDownload  INTEGER, 
        ipUnityAnncInstAction           INTEGER, 
	ipUnityAnncInstPath	        DisplayString,
	ipUnityAnncInstLanguageOption1	LanguageBitMap,
	ipUnityAnncInstLanguageOption2	LanguageBitMap,
	ipUnityAnncInstLanguageOption3	LanguageBitMap,
	ipUnityAnncInstRowStatus	RowStatus
	}  

ipUnityAnncInstIndex	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Index for this table."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 1 }

ipUnityAnncInstSectionType	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		critical (0),
		permanent (1),
                userChange (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Announcement instruction section type for this announcement instruction.This object
                 is used to indicate to the user as to which section the entry belongs to."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 2 }

ipUnityAnncInstDesignation	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		critical (0),
		permanent (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Announcement instruction designation." 
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 3 }

ipUnityAnncInstType	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		system (0),
		application (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Announcement instruction type." 
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 4 }    

ipUnityAnncInstDynamicDownload	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		off (0),
		on (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
                  "Denotes whether the main directory is defined to be a 
                   dynamically downloadable path or not. Only PERMANENT 
                   announcement directories can be configured as 
                   dynamically downloadable."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 5 }    

ipUnityAnncInstAction	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		none (0),
		remove  (1),
		update  (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The row in the user config can be marked as remove. This row will be removed when save 
                 operation is done using anncInstCommand. Similarly the critical or permananet row can be marked as 
                 remove which will be removed in the similar way.
                 If user add or replace the audio files,  particular instruction entry needs to be reloaded by the bank. 
                 On setting the entry to update will reload the specified entry." 
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 6 }    

ipUnityAnncInstPath	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
                "Root directory of inventory of announcements. Actual download can be from this directory or sub directories                  within this directory." 
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 7 }    

ipUnityAnncInstLanguageOption1 OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX LanguageBitMap 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"This identifies the languages to be downloaded.This value has to be compulsorily set."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 8 }    

ipUnityAnncInstLanguageOption2 OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX LanguageBitMap 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"This identifies the languages to be downloaded. This object is optional and need not be set
                 along with the other objects."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 9 }    

ipUnityAnncInstLanguageOption3 OBJECT-TYPE

	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"This identifies the languages to be downloaded.This object is optional and need not be set
		 along with the other objects."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 10 }    

ipUnityAnncInstRowStatus	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX RowStatus 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The status of the row. Required to create or delete the entry in 
		this table. Only createAndGo method of row creation is supported 
		and createAndWait method is not supported. Actual
                deletion happens when user does the save operation using anncInstCommand."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstEntry 11 }    

ipUnityAnncInstFileNextIndex		OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Identifies a hint for the next value of anncInstFileIndex to 
		be used in a row creation attempt for the anncInstFileTable. 
		If no new rows can be created, this object will have a value
		of -1."
	::= { ipUnityAnncConfig 5 }		

ipUnityAnncInstFileTable		OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityAnncInstFileEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The table is used to add and delete the files in the User 
                 Changes announcement instruction entries. A file can be added or 
                deleted for those rows created in the annInstTable in the user 
                Config section."
	::= { ipUnityAnncConfig 6 }

ipUnityAnncInstFileEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IpUnityAnncInstFileEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"An entry for announcement instruction file."
    INDEX      { ipUnityAnncInstIndex,ipUnityAnncInstFileIndex }
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstFileTable 1 }

IpUnityAnncInstFileEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityAnncInstFileIndex	Integer32,
	ipUnityAnncInstFileSectionType	INTEGER,
	ipUnityAnncInstFileName	        DisplayString,
	ipUnityAnncInstFileRowStatus	RowStatus
	}  

ipUnityAnncInstFileIndex	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Index for this table."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstFileEntry 1 }

ipUnityAnncInstFileSectionType	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		critical (0),
		permanent (1),
                userChange (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Announcement instruction file section type for this announcement instruction.This object
                 is used to indicate to the user as to which section the file belongs to."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstFileEntry 2 }

ipUnityAnncInstFileName	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
                "The name of the audio file."
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstFileEntry 3 }    

ipUnityAnncInstFileRowStatus	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX RowStatus 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The status of the row. Required to create or delete the entry in 
		this table. Only createAndGo method of row creation is supported 
		and createAndWait method is not supported. Delete method will delete the file
                in the user changes section. Deleteion of files is not allowed if the
                entry is in critical or permanent section." 
    ::= { ipUnityAnncInstFileEntry 4 }    

ipUnityAnncInstCommand	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		save (1),
		cancel (2)
	} 
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	       "Command for announcement instructions
		save (1) - This applys to the announcement instructions created 
		           in the anncInstTable and anncInstFileTable. 
                           It also removes the entries for
		           critical and permanent announcement instructuion entries if they 
		           are marked as removed(1).
		cancel (2) - This  will remove all the user changes before the save command and also will 
                             change the critical or permanent entires marked as removed(1) to none(0)" 
    ::= { ipUnityAnncConfig 7 }

		when all the odsp banks are OutOfService."

	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

    ::= { evEntry 2 }

		active (1),
		toBeRemoved (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF UserEvEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current

	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		save (1),
		cancelDelete (2)
	} 
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Command for embedded variable
		
		save (1) - This applys the embedded variables created 
		           in the userEvTable. It also removes the entries from
		           evTable if they are marked as ToBeRemoved (2).
		           
		cancelDelete (2) - This marks the embedded variable that are
		                   marked as toBeRemoved (2) to active (1) in
		                   evTable"
    ::= { evConfig 3 }

-- snmpConfig group objects
snmpNextManagerNum		OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32(0..4 | -1)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Identifies a hint for the next value of snmpManagerNum to 
		be used in a row creation attempt for the snmpManagerTable. 
		If no new rows can be created, this object will have a value
		of 0."
	::= { snmpConfig 1 }
	
snmpManagerTable		OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF SnmpManagerEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The table is used for configuring SNMP Managers. This table serves
		as traps destination table. MediaServer sends all the SNMP traps to 
		configured SNMP Managers in this table."
	::= { snmpConfig 2 }

snmpManagerEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SnmpManagerEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"An entry for each SNMP Manager (trap destination)."
    INDEX { snmpManagerNum }
    ::= { snmpManagerTable 1 }

SnmpManagerEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	snmpManagerNum			Integer32,
	snmpTrapDestAddress		DisplayString,
	snmpTrapPort			Integer32,
	snmpTrapCommunityString		DisplayString, 
	snmpManagerAccess		INTEGER,
	snmpManagerRowStatus	RowStatus
	}  
	
snmpManagerNum	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32(0..4)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"SNMP Manager number."
    ::= { snmpManagerEntry 1 }

snmpTrapDestAddress	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Hostname or the IP Address of the trap destination."
    ::= { snmpManagerEntry 2 }
    
snmpTrapPort OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32(162 | 1025..65535)
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Port to send the SNMP traps for this manager. This object is not
		mandatory to create the row in this table. If value is not provided
		then 162 will be used as trap port."
	DEFVAL {162}
    ::= { snmpManagerEntry 3 }
    
snmpTrapCommunityString OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString (SIZE(1..32))
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Community string used in the trap message for this manager. This 
		object is not mandatory to create the row in this table. If value 
		is not provided then public will be used as trap community string."
	DEFVAL {"public"}
    ::= { snmpManagerEntry 4 }

snmpManagerAccess OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
	  trap (1),
	  set (2),
	  trapAndSet (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Access for this SNMP manager. If it is Trap then manager receives
		Traps and can perform get operation. If it TrapAndSet then manager
		can perform set operation. This is two restrict the number of
		SNMP managers that perform set operation and adds security in
		case of SNMPv2c."
	DEFVAL {1}
    ::= { snmpManagerEntry 5 }    

snmpManagerRowStatus    OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX RowStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The status of the row. Required to create or delete the entry in 
		this table. Only createAndGo method of row creation is supported 
		and createAndWait method is not supported."
	::= { snmpManagerEntry 6 }    
    
-- fax configuration related objects
	 
faxRate OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32 ( 2400 | 4800 | 7200 | 9600 | 12000 | 14400)
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Used for configuring fax rate."
	::= { faxConfig 1 }

faxPayloadSize OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX OCTET STRING (SIZE(1..3))
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Used for configuring fax payload size. Take upto three bytes and each 
                 byte takes decimal value of 10, 20 or 30. Same value can not be
                 repeasted. Some examples in decimal values of the bytes are
                 a) 10 b) 20 10 30 c) 20 30 d) 10 20 30
                
                 Same examples when represeneted in Hex
                 a) 0a b) 14 0a 1e c) 14 1e d) 0a 14 1e"
               
	DEFVAL {'14'h}
	::= { faxConfig 2 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarNextIndex		OBJECT-TYPE

ipUnityEmbeddedVarTable		OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IpUnityEmbeddedVarEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The table is used for creating change section entries and  
                 viewing commit section. Same table is also used to remove the entries,
		 however user can only mark the entries to remove. Actual
		 deletion happens when user does the save operation using ipUnityEmbeddedVarCommand."
	::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarConfig 2 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IpUnityEmbeddedVarEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
		"An entry for Embedded variables."
    INDEX      { ipUnityEmbeddedVarIndex }
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarTable 1 }

IpUnityEmbeddedVarEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ipUnityEmbeddedVarIndex	        Integer32,
	ipUnityEmbeddedVarAction	INTEGER,
	ipUnityEmbeddedVarSectionType	INTEGER,
	ipUnityEmbeddedVarIdString      DisplayString,
	ipUnityEmbeddedVarExpString	DisplayString,
	ipUnityEmbeddedVarRowStatus	RowStatus
	}  

ipUnityEmbeddedVarIndex	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Index for this table."
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry 1 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarAction	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		nothing (0),
		removed (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Embedded variable action value for this entry. This object
                 is used to delete the entry in the user changes."
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry 2 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarSectionType	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		commit (0),
		change (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Embedded variable section type for this entry. This object
                 is used to indicate to the user as to which section the entry belongs to."
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry 3 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarIdString	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString (SIZE(1..100))
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Embedded variable ID string."
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry 4 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarExpString	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX DisplayString (SIZE(1..100))
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Embedded variable expression string."
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry 5 }

ipUnityEmbeddedVarRowStatus	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX RowStatus 
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"The status of the row. Required to create or delete the entry in 
		this table. Only createAndGo method of row creation is supported 
		and createAndWait method is not supported. Actual
                deletion happens when user does the save operation using ipUnityEmbeddedVarCommand."
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarEntry 6 }    

ipUnityEmbeddedVarCommand	OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		save (1),
		cancel (2)
	} 
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
	       "Command for Embedded variable,
		save (1) - This applys to the embeded variable created 
		           in the ipUnityEmbeddedVar table. It also removes the entries  
		           if they are marked as removed(1).
		cancel (2) - This  will remove all the user changes before the save command and also will 
                             chnage the commit section entires marked as removed(1) to none(0). " 
    ::= { ipUnityEmbeddedVarConfig 3 }

-- IP Sec Transform table

	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

	::= { ipsec 6 }

    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION

	ipSecTransformIndex		Integer32,
	encryption				INTEGER,
	authentication			INTEGER,
	protocol				INTEGER,
	ipSecTransformNumber			Integer32,
	ipSecTransformRowStatus	RowStatus
	}

	SYNTAX Integer32(0..6)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Index for this table."
    ::= { ipSecTransformEntry 1 }

		des (2),
		des3 (3),
		null (11)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION
		"IP Sec Transform encryption:  des, des3, null"
    ::= { ipSecTransformEntry 2 }

	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		md5 (1),
		sha (2)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current
	DESCRIPTION

	::= { ipSecTransformEntry 3 }

	SYNTAX INTEGER {
		esp (1)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-create
	STATUS current

	MAX-ACCESS read-only

-- IP Sec Ethernet Interface Mode table

    SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF IPSecEtherModeEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
        "The table is used for configuring IP Sec Ethernet Interface Mode."
    ::= { ipsec 7 }

ipSecEtherModeEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX IPSecEtherModeEntry
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
        "An entry for IP Sec Ethernet Interface Mode. One entry per card
         and per interface."
    INDEX      { etherInterface }
    ::= { ipSecEtherModeTable 1 }

IPSecEtherModeEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
    etherInterface           Integer32,
    etherMode                        INTEGER
    }
   
etherInterface   OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX Integer32 (0..7)
    MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
        "Ethernet Interface number to set the Mode:  0-7."
    ::= { ipSecEtherModeEntry 1 }

etherMode    OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX INTEGER {
        off (0),
        on (1)
    }
    MAX-ACCESS read-write
    STATUS current
    DESCRIPTION
        "Mode for configured Ethernet Interface:  off or on. If a
        particular interface is on then automatically it becomes
        off for other interface. Only one interface can be turned on
        per card."
    DEFVAL {off}
    ::= { ipSecEtherModeEntry 2 }

-- IP Unity notifications : classified into SCC, ODSP and "other" categories 
-- and the notifications are numbered according to the category they belong to 
-- with some scope left for adding more in the same class : so, although the V1 trap
-- numbers remain the same, the corresponding V2 notifications now have entirely
-- different numbers.


--
-- SCC "Critical" Notifications
--


ipUnitySccCpuOverload	NOTIFICATION-TYPE
	OBJECTS	{ ipUnityTrapSeverity, ipUnityCardIndex, ipUnityTrapInfoString, ipUnitySequenceNumber }
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION " the CPU usage is high in the SCC ."
        ::= { ipUnityNotifications 7 }

ipUnitySccTaskSuspended	 NOTIFICATION-TYPE
        OBJECTS  { ipUnityTrapSeverity, ipUnityCardIndex, ipUnitySccTaskName, ipUnityTrapInfoString, ipUnitySequenceNumber }
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION " a task in the SCC gets suspended."
        ::= { ipUnityNotifications 8 }

ipUnitySccNoMateAlarm      NOTIFICATION-TYPE
        OBJECTS  { ipUnityTrapSeverity, ipUnityCardIndex,ipUnityCardType, ipUnityTrapInfoString, ipUnitySequenceNumber }
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION " the SCC does not have a mate card."
        ::= { ipUnityNotifications 14 }

ipUnitySccSwitchOverFailure	 NOTIFICATION-TYPE
        OBJECTS { ipUnityTrapSeverity, ipUnityCardIndex, ipUnityTrapInfoString, ipUnitySequenceNumber }
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION " the SCC's switchover to the backup SCC has failed ."
        ::= { ipUnityNotifications 17 }

ipUnityDataSyncFailure     NOTIFICATION-TYPE
        OBJECTS { ipUnityTrapSeverity, ipUnityCardIndex, ipUnityTrapInfoString, ipUnitySequenceNumber }
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION " the data synchronization fails between the SCCs."
        ::= { ipUnityNotifications 19 }

ipUnitySccTaskResumeFailed	NOTIFICATION-TYPE
        OBJECTS  { ipUnityTrapSeverity, ipUnityCardIndex , ipUnitySccTaskName, ipUnityTrapInfoString, ipUnitySequenceNumber }
        STATUS      current
        DESCRIPTION " a task resumption fails in the SCC."
